---
layout: "post"
permalink: /stlc-agda/
title: "Simple Typed Lambda Calculus In Agda"
date: "2018-08-17"
categories: type-theory home
toc: true
agda: true
latex: true
---

We present a formalisation of the syntax in Agda for the *Simple Typed Lambda
Calculus (STLC)* with some of its properties and the description of the
type-checking for this type system. We refactor the implementation by
[@gergoerdi](https://github.com/gergoerdi/stlc-agda/) for this calculus,
in particular the [Scopecheck](https://github.com/jonaprieto/stlctalk/blob/master/src/Scopecheck.agda)
and [Typecheck](https://github.com/jonaprieto/stlctalk/blob/master/src/Typecheck.agda) module.

The following source code was tested with:

- Agda v2.5.4
- Agda Standard Library v0.16

The original content was firstly exposed in the seminar of logic at Universidad EAFIT.

  - [Slides](https://github.com/jonaprieto/stlctalk/raw/master/slides/slides.pdf).
  - Repository: [https://github.com/jonaprieto/stlctalk](https://github.com/jonaprieto/stlctalk).

{: .foldable }

### Bound

Lambda terms using De Bruijn indexes.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="2091" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Bound"></a><a id="2098" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2098" class="Module">Bound</a> <a id="2104" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2105" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2105" class="Bound">Type</a> <a id="2110" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2112" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="2115" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2117" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="2126" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="2131" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="2138" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Nat.html" class="Module">Data.Nat</a>    <a id="2150" class="Keyword">hiding</a> <a id="2157" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2158" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Nat.Base.html#2869" class="Function Operator">_≟_</a><a id="2161" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="2298" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="S"></a><a id="2305" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2305" class="Module">S</a> <a id="2307" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="2309" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1399" class="Module">Syntax</a> <a id="2316" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2105" class="Bound">Type</a>

Syntax using indexes.

      <a id="3180" class="Comment">------------------------------</a>
      <a id="3217" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3219" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3137" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="3221" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2771" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="3223" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1536" class="InductiveConstructor">lam</a> <a id="3227" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3228" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3126" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="3230" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1456" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∶</a> <a id="3232" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3128" class="Bound">A</a><a id="3233" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3235" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3130" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="3237" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2771" class="Datatype Operator">⇝</a> <a id="3239" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2475" class="InductiveConstructor">lam</a> <a id="3243" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3128" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3245" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3132" class="Bound">t&#39;</a>

### Scopecheck

Check representation of λ-terms using de Bruijn indexes.
Get a λ-term using de Bruijn indexes by given a λ-term with names.

{: .foldable }
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="4319" class="Comment">-- ∃-syntax and ∄-syntax</a>

    <a id="5941" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5943" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5944" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5944" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="5946" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5948" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2645" class="Function">Binder</a> <a id="5955" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5934" class="Bound">n</a><a id="5956" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5958" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5960" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5961" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5961" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="5963" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5965" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1366" class="Function">Name</a><a id="5969" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="5975" class="Comment">------------------------------</a>
    <a id="6010" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6012" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#534" class="Datatype">Dec</a> <a id="6016" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6017" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#4462" class="Function">∃[</a> <a id="6020" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6020" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="6022" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#4462" class="Function">]</a> <a id="6024" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6025" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5944" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="6027" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2771" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="6029" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1512" class="InductiveConstructor">var</a> <a id="6033" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5961" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="6035" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2771" class="Datatype Operator">⇝</a> <a id="6037" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6020" class="Bound">t</a><a id="6038" class="Symbol">))</a>

              <a id="6732" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="6737" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5320" class="Function">name-dec</a> <a id="6746" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6706" class="Bound">Γ,y⊢varx⇝t</a>
            <a id="6769" class="Symbol">...</a>  <a id="6774" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="6776" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#470" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₁</a> <a id="6781" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6781" class="Bound">x≡y</a>                    <a id="6804" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6806" class="Bound">x≢y</a> <a id="6810" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6781" class="Bound">x≡y</a>
            <a id="6826" class="Symbol">...</a>  <a id="6831" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="6833" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#495" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₂</a> <a id="6838" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6838" class="Bound">p</a><a id="6839" class="Symbol">@(</a><a id="6841" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6841" class="Bound">t′</a> <a id="6844" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">-by-</a> <a id="6849" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6849" class="Bound">Γ⊢varx⇝t′</a><a id="6858" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6860" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6862" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6590" class="Bound">∄t⟨Γ⊢varx⇝t⟩</a> <a id="6875" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6838" class="Bound">p</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

We want to determine if given a variable context and a term,
it is possible to find its encoding using De Bruijn indexes.
If so, we got its respective construction for that lambda term.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="Scopecheck.check"></a><a id="7091" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7091" class="Function">check</a>
    <a id="7101" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7103" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="7105" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7106" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7106" class="Bound">n</a><a id="7107" class="Symbol">}</a>
    <a id="7113" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7115" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7116" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7116" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="7118" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7120" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2645" class="Function">Binder</a> <a id="7127" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7106" class="Bound">n</a><a id="7128" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="7134" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7136" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7137" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7137" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="7139" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7141" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1491" class="Datatype">S.Expr</a><a id="7147" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="7153" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7155" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#534" class="Datatype">Dec</a> <a id="7159" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7160" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#4462" class="Function">∃[</a> <a id="7163" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7163" class="Bound">t′</a> <a id="7166" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#4462" class="Function">]</a> <a id="7168" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7169" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7116" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="7171" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2771" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="7173" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7137" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="7175" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2771" class="Datatype Operator">⇝</a> <a id="7177" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7163" class="Bound">t′</a><a id="7179" class="Symbol">))</a>

  <a id="7185" class="Comment">-- By induction on the term syntax.</a>

  <a id="8711" class="Comment">-- Go from a representation that uses Names to one that uses de Bruijn indices</a>
  <a id="Scopecheck.scope"></a><a id="8792" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8792" class="Function">scope</a> <a id="8798" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8800" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8801" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8801" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="8803" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8805" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1491" class="Datatype">S.Expr</a><a id="8811" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8813" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8815" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8816" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8816" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="8818" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8820" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.Decidable.html#897" class="Function">True</a> <a id="8825" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8826" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7091" class="Function">check</a> <a id="8832" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Vec.html#712" class="InductiveConstructor">[]</a> <a id="8835" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8801" class="Bound">t</a><a id="8836" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="8839" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8841" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2420" class="Datatype">Expr</a> <a id="8846" class="Number">0</a>
  <a id="8850" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8792" class="Function">scope</a> <a id="8856" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8856" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="8858" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8859" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8859" class="Bound">p</a><a id="8860" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8862" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8864" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#155" class="Field">proj₁</a> <a id="8870" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8871" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.Decidable.html#1055" class="Function">toWitness</a> <a id="8881" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8859" class="Bound">p</a><a id="8882" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

    <a id="10577" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#10513" class="Function">K</a> <a id="10579" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10581" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#9982" class="InductiveConstructor">tLam</a> <a id="10586" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10587" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#9982" class="InductiveConstructor">tLam</a> <a id="10592" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#9916" class="InductiveConstructor">tVar</a><a id="10596" class="Symbol">)</a>

    <a id="10603" class="Keyword">postulate</a>
      <a id="Typing.A"></a><a id="10619" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#10619" class="Postulate">A</a> <a id="10621" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10623" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#9505" class="Datatype">Type</a>
      <a id="Typing.B"></a><a id="10634" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#10634" class="Postulate">B</a> <a id="10636" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10638" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#9505" class="Datatype">Type</a>
      <a id="Typing.C"></a><a id="10649" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#10649" class="Postulate">C</a> <a id="10651" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10653" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#9505" class="Datatype">Type</a>

    <a id="10663" class="Comment">-- S : [] ⊢ lam (A ↣ (B ↣ C))</a>
    <a id="10697" class="Comment">--              (lam (A ↣ B)</a>
    <a id="10730" class="Comment">--                   (lam A</a>
    <a id="10762" class="Comment">--                     ((var (# 2)) ∙ (var (# 0))) ∙ ((var (# 1)) ∙ (var (# 0))) ))</a>
    <a id="10850" class="Comment">--        ∶ (A ↣ (B ↣ C)) ↣ (A ↣ B) ↣ A ↣ C</a>
    <a id="10898" class="Comment">-- S = tLam (tLam ((tLam ({! tVar  !} ∙ {!   !})) ∙ ({! tVar  !} ∙ {!   !}))) --  tLam (tLam (tLam ((tVar ∙ tVar) ∙ (tVar ∙ tVar))))</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

### References
